        <script type="text/javascript">
         // Set the date we're counting down to
var countDownDate = new Date("Jun 25, 2018 19:00:00").getTime();

// Update the count down every 1 second
var x = setInterval(function() {

    // Get todays date and time
    var now = new Date().getTime();
    
    // Find the distance between now an the count down date
    var distance = countDownDate - now ;
    
    // Time calculations for days, hours, minutes and seconds
    var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
	var sdays = "";
    var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
	var shours = "";
    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
	var sminutes = "";
    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);
	var sseconds = "";
	
	if (days <10)
		sdays = "0"+ days;
	else
		sdays = days;

	if (hours <10)
		shours = "0"+ hours;
	else
		shours = hours;

	if (minutes <10)
		sminutes = "0"+ minutes;
	else
		sminutes = minutes;

	if (seconds <10)
		sseconds = "0"+ seconds;
	else
		sseconds = seconds;
		
    // Output the result in an element with id="countdown"
    //document.getElementById("countdown").innerHTML = "Geri Sayım "
    document.getElementById("countdays").innerHTML =  sdays ;
    document.getElementById("counthours").innerHTML =  shours ;
    document.getElementById("countminutes").innerHTML =  sminutes ;
    document.getElementById("countseconds").innerHTML =  sseconds ;

    
    // If the count down is over, write some text 
    if (distance < 0) {
        clearInterval(x);
        document.getElementById("countdown").style.visibility='hidden';
      document.getElementById("countdown").style.height = '0px';
    }
}, 1000);

                 <div class="sfTxtContent" id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl2_SimpleImageField1_ctl00_ctl00_textLabel_read">

                </div>
                <a href="detay/2018/05/12/basketbol-gen%C3%A7ler-ligi-nde-%C5%9Fampiyon-anadolu-efes" id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl2_DetailsViewHyperLink1">
                 Basketbol Gençler Ligi’nde Şampiyon: Anadolu Efes
                </a>
                <div class="sfnewsSummary">
                 Basketbol Gençler Ligi Dörtlü Finali’nde Darüşşafaka Basketbol’u 81-71 skorla mağlup eden Anadolu Efes şampiyonluğa ulaştı.
                </div>
               </li>
               <li>
                <div id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl3_SimpleImageField1">
                 <div class="sfTxtContent" id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl3_SimpleImageField1_ctl00_ctl00_textLabel_read">
                 </div>
                 <img id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl3_SimpleImageField1_ctl00_ctl00_image" src="http://cdn.tbf.org.tr/Media/images/default-source/Genel/basketbolgenclerligi_25092017_0001_300x300.jpg?sfvrsn=0"/>
                </div>
                <a href="detay/2018/05/12/fenerbah%C3%A7e-do%C4%9Fu%C5%9F-basketbol-gen%C3%A7ler-ligi-ni-%C3%BC%C3%A7%C3%BCnc%C3%BC-s%C4%B1rada-tamamlad%C4%B1" id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl3_DetailsViewHyperLink1">
                 Fenerbahçe Doğuş Basketbol Gençler Ligi’ni Üçüncü Sırada Tamamladı
                </a>
                <div class="sfnewsSummary">
                 Sinan Erdem Spor Salonu’nun ev sahipliğinde gerçekleştirilen Basketbol Gençler Ligi’nde Banvit’i 82-81’lik skorla mağlup eden Fenerbahçe Doğuş, üçüncü oldu.
                </div>
               </li>
               <li>
                <div id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl4_SimpleImageField1">
                 <div class="sfTxtContent" id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl4_SimpleImageField1_ctl00_ctl00_textLabel_read">
                 </div>
                 <img id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl4_SimpleImageField1_ctl00_ctl00_image" src="http://cdn.tbf.org.tr/Media/images/default-source/Genel/basketbolgenclerligi_25092017_0001_300x300.jpg?sfvrsn=0"/>
                </div>
                <a href="detay/2018/05/11/basketbol-gen%C3%A7ler-ligi-nde-finalin-ad%C4%B1-dar%C3%BC%C5%9F%C5%9Fafaka-basketbol-andolu-efes" id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl4_DetailsViewHyperLink1">
                 Basketbol Gençler Ligi’nde Finalin Adı: Darüşşafaka Basketbol – Anadolu Efes
                </a>
                <div class="sfnewsSummary">
                 Sinan Erdem Spor Salonu’nun ev sahipliğinde gerçekleştirilen Basketbol Gençler Ligi’nde oynanan yarı final karşılaşmalarının ardından Darüşşafaka Basketbol ile Anadolu Efes finale yükseldi.
                </div>
               </li>
               <li>
                <div id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl5_SimpleImageField1">
                 <div class="sfTxtContent" id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl5_SimpleImageField1_ctl00_ctl00_textLabel_read">

                </div>
                <a href="detay/2018/05/11/anadolu-efes-basketbol-gen%C3%A7ler-ligi-nde-finale-y%C3%BCkseldi" id="ctl00_contentPlaceholder_C272_newsFrontendList_ctl00_ctl00_NewsList_ctrl5_DetailsViewHyperLink1">
                 Anadolu Efes, Basketbol Gençler Ligi’nde Finale Yükseldi
                </a>
                <div class="sfnewsSummary">
                 Sinan Erdem Spor Salonu’nun ev sahipliğinde gerçekleştirilen Basketbol Gençler Ligi’nin yarı final mücadelesinde Anadolu Efes, Fenerbahçe Doğuş’u 86-68’lik skorla mağlup etti.
                </div>
               </li>
              </ul>

             function radMenuOnClick(sender, args) {

        var state = args.get_item().get_attributes().getAttribute("ExpandOnClick");
        args.get_item().get_attributes().setAttribute("ExpandOnClick", "true")
        args.get_item().open();
    }

    function radMenuOnOpening(sender, args) {
        var state = args.get_item().get_attributes().getAttribute("ExpandOnClick");
        if(state != "true")
            args.set_cancel(true);
        args.get_item().get_attributes().setAttribute("ExpandOnClick", "false")
    }
